RawQuerySet (line 2210) stores these separately and passes them to RawQuery (django/db/models/sql/query.py:150), which executes the query through the _execute_query() method.\\n\\n**Critical Parameter Adaptation Layer:**\\nRawQuery._execute_query() (django/db/models/sql/query.py:203-220) is the critical SQL injection prevention point for raw() queries. It:\\n1. Gets the database connection via connections[self.using]\\n2. Calls connection.ops.adapt_unknown_value() on each parameter to adapt Python types to database driver types (lines 209-217)\\n3. Preserves parameter separation and passes both to cursor.execute()\\n\\nThe adapt_unknown_value() method (django/db/backends/base/operations.py:550-567) provides type-specific parameter adaptation for datetime, date, time, decimal, and other types, preventing type-based SQL injection. Each database backend (PostgreSQL, MySQL, SQLite, Oracle) overrides this with database-specific adaptations.\\n\\n**Cursor Execution Layer:**\\nCursorWrapper (django/db/backends/utils.py:17) is the central enforcement point for all database queries. The execute() method (line 78) and executemany() method (line 83) route through _execute_with_wrappers() (line 88), which chains execution wrappers before calling _execute() or _executemany().\\n\\nThe _execute() method (line 94) enforces parameterized execution by:\\n1. Validating transaction state\\n2. Calling cursor.execute(sql) with params=None (line 103) or cursor.execute(sql, params) (line 105) separately\\n\\nThis separation of SQL and parameters is enforced at the database driver level through PEP 249 parameterized query support.\\n\\n**Identifier Escaping:**\\nThe quote_name() method in BaseDatabaseOperations (django/db/backends/base/operations.py:413) and backend-specific implementations quote all identifiers (table names, column names, index names) with database-specific quoting, preventing SQL injection through identifier manipulation.\\n\\n**Extra Query Parameters:**\\nThe QuerySet.extra() method (django/db/models/query.py:1876) uses ExtraWhere (django/db/models/sql/where.py:334) to handle extra() clause parameters. The as_sql() method (line 343) wraps each SQL fragment and maintains the parameter list separately.\\n\\n**Complete Parameter Chain:**\\nAll query compilation flows through SQLCompiler (django/db/models/sql/compiler.py), which builds parameterized SQL using Value expressions (django/db/models/expressions.py:1144) that maintain parameter separation. Field.get_db_prep_value() (django/db/models/fields/__init__.py:996) and get_db_prep_save() (line 1007) prepare field values through the same parameter adaptation pipeline.\\n\\nDjango's multi-layered approach ensures SQL injection prevention at every level: expression building (RawSQL, Value), query compilation (SQLCompiler), parameter adaptation (adapt_unknown_value), and cursor execution (CursorWrapper), with database backend-specific implementations for each supported database.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
